# NI DOCUMENT BUNDLE: rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref

<!--NI_BUNDLE_CHUNK bundle=rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref start=1 end=250 -->
<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/configuration/dir-mnu.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00001: Configuration

- bundle_id: `rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/configuration/dir-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/configuration/dir-mnu.html
- document_id: `rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the VIs on this palette to configure various parameters for RFmxBT measurements. icon

### Configuration

Use the VIs on this palette to configure various parameters for RFmxBT measurements.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='dir-mnu.png']

- [RFmxBT Configure RF VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-configure-rf-vi.html) Configures the RF properties of the signal specified by the selector string.
- [RFmxBT Configure Frequency VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-configure-frequency-vi.html) Configures the expected carrier frequency of the RF signal to acquire. The signal analyzer tunes to this frequency.
- [RFmxBT Configure Reference Level VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-configure-reference-level-vi.html) Configures the reference level which represents the maximum expected power of an RF input signal.
- [RFmxBT Configure External Attenuation VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-configure-external-attenuation-vi.html) Configures the attenuation of a switch (or cable) connected to the RF IN connector of the signal analyzer.
- [RFmxBT Auto Level VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-auto-level-vi.html) Examines the input signal to calculate the peak power level and sets it as the value of the Reference Level property. Use this VI to help calculate an approximate setting for the reference level.
- [RFmxBT Auto Detect Signal VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-auto-detect-signal-vi.html) Detects the Bluetooth packet and returns the detected packet type, data rate, and payload length.
- [RFmxBT Configure Trigger VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-configure-trigger-vi.html) Configures the reference trigger to use to acquire the signal.
- [RFmxBT Send Software Edge Trigger VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-send-software-edge-trigger-vi.html) Sends a trigger to the device when you use the RFmxBT Configure Trigger VI to choose a software version of a trigger and the device is waiting for the trigger to be sent. You can also use this VI to override a hardware trigger.
- [RFmxBT Configure Packet Type VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-configure-packet-type-vi.html) Configures the type of Bluetooth packet to be measured.
- [RFmxBT Configure Data Rate VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-configure-data-rate-vi.html) Configures the data rate of low energy (LE) or low energy - channel sounding (LE-CS) packets to be measured.
- [RFmxBT Configure Payload Bit Pattern VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-configure-payload-bit-pattern-vi.html) Configures the bit pattern present in the payload of the packet.
- [RFmxBT Configure Payload Length VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-configure-payload-length-vi.html) Configures the Payload Length Mode and Payload Length parameters that decide the length of the payload to be used for the measurement.
- [RFmxBT Configure LE Direction Finding VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-configure-le-direction-finding-vi.html) Configures the mode of direction finding, length of the constant tone extension field, and the duration of the switching slot in the generated signal.
- [RFmxBT Configure Channel Number VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-configure-channel-number-vi.html) Configures the RF channel number of the signal generated by the device under test (DUT), as defined in the Bluetooth specification.
- [ModAcc](../../../../../../menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/configuration/rfmx-bt-mx-configuration-modacc-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to configure modulation accuracy (ModAcc) measurements. You can also use the RFmxBT Property Node to configure additional properties.
- [ACP](../../../../../../menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/configuration/rfmx-bt-mx-configuration-acp-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to configure ACP measurements. You can use the RFmxBT Property Node to configure additional properties.
- [20dBBandwidth](../../../../../../menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/configuration/rfmx-bt-mx-configuration-20dbbandwidth-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to configure the 20dBBandwidth measurements. You can also use the RFmxBT Property Node to configure additional properties.
- [Frequency Range](../../../../../../menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/configuration/rfmx-bt-mx-configuration-frequencyrange-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to configure the Frequency Range measurements. You can also use the RFmxBT Property Node to configure additional properties.
- [TXP](../../../../../../menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/configuration/rfmx-bt-mx-configuration-txp-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to configure transmit power (TXP) measurements. You can also use the RFmxBT Property Node to configure additional properties.
- [PowerRamp](../../../../../../menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/configuration/rfmx-bt-mx-configuration-powerramp-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to configure PowerRamp measurements. You can use the RFmxBT Property Node to configure additional properties.
- [ModSpectrum](../../../../../../menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/configuration/rfmx-bt-mx-configuration-modspectrum-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to configure ModSpectrum measurements. You can use the RFmxBT Property Node to configure additional properties.

Parent topic:

Bluetooth

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/configuration/rfmx-bt-mx-configuration-20dbbandwidth-mnu.html language=enus -->

### 20dBBandwidth

Use the VIs on this palette to configure the 20dBBandwidth measurements. You can also use the RFmxBT Property Node to configure additional properties.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='rfmx-bt-mx-configuration-20dbbandwidth-mnu.png']

- [RFmxBT 20dBBandwidth Configure Averaging VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-20dbbandwidth-configure-averaging-vi.html) Configures averaging for the 20dBBandwidth measurement.

Parent topic:

Configuration

## TOPIC 00003: ACP

- bundle_id: `rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/configuration/rfmx-bt-mx-configuration-acp-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/configuration/rfmx-bt-mx-configuration-acp-mnu.html
- document_id: `rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the VIs on this palette to configure ACP measurements. You can use the RFmxBT Property Node to configure additional properties. icon

### ACP

Use the VIs on this palette to configure ACP measurements. You can use the RFmxBT Property Node to configure additional properties.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='rfmx-bt-mx-configuration-acp-mnu.png']

- [RFmxBT ACP Configure Averaging VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-acp-configure-averaging-vi.html) Configures averaging for the adjacent channel power (ACP) measurement.
- [RFmxBT ACP Configure Burst Synchronization Type VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-acp-configure-burst-synchronization-type-vi.html) Configures the type of synchronization used for detecting the start of the packet in the adjacent channel power (ACP) measurement.
- [RFmxBT ACP Configure Offset Channel Mode VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-acp-configure-offset-channel-mode-vi.html) Configures the offset channels used for the adjacent channel power (ACP) measurement.
- [RFmxBT ACP Configure Number of Offsets VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-acp-configure-number-of-offsets-vi.html) Configures the number of offsets for the adjacent channel power (ACP) measurement.

Parent topic:

Configuration

## TOPIC 00009: Bluetooth

- bundle_id: `rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/dir-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/dir-mnu.html
- document_id: `rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the VIs on this palette to perform Bluetooth measurements. You can use the RFmxBT Property Node to configure additional properties. © 2019–2026 National Instruments Corporation. All rights reserved. icon

### Bluetooth

Use the VIs on this palette to perform Bluetooth measurements. You can use the [RFmxBT Property Node](/csh?context=rfmxbt_rfmxbtvi_rfmxbt_property_node) to configure additional properties.

© 2019–2026 National Instruments Corporation. All rights reserved.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='dir-mnu.png']

- [Configuration](../../../../../menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/configuration/dir-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to configure various parameters for RFmxBT measurements.
- [RFmxBT Select Measurement VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-select-measurement-vi.html) Specifies the measurements that you want to enable. To select a single measurement, use the Single Measurement instance. To select multiple measurements, use the Multiple Measurements instance.
- [RFmxBT Initiate VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-initiate-vi.html) Initiates all enabled measurements. Call this VI after configuring the signal and measurement. This VI asynchronously launches measurements in the background and immediately returns to the caller program. You can fetch measurement results using the Fetch VIs or result properties in the property node. To get the status of measurements, use the RFmxBT Wait for Measurement Complete VI or RFmxBT Check Measurement Status VI.
- [Fetch](../../../../../menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/rfmx-bt-mx-fetch-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to fetch Bluetooth measurement results and traces.
- [Utility](../../../../../menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/utility/dir-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to configure utility VIs.
- [RFmxBT Property Node VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-property-node-vi.html) Gets (reads), sets (writes), or resets (sets to default value) RFmxBluetooth properties.
- [Advanced](../../../../../menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/rfmx-bt-mx-advanced-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to use advanced features.
- [Build String](../../../../../menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/utility/rfmx-bt-mx-utility-build-string-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to create strings for configurations and results that require a selector string.

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/rfmx-bt-mx-advanced-mnu.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00010: Advanced

- bundle_id: `rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/rfmx-bt-mx-advanced-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/rfmx-bt-mx-advanced-mnu.html
- document_id: `rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the VIs on this palette to use advanced features. icon

### Advanced

Use the VIs on this palette to use advanced features.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='rfmx-bt-mx-advanced-mnu.png']

- [RFmxBT Abort Measurements VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-abort-measurements-vi.html) Stops acquisition and measurements associated with signal instance that you specify in the Selector String parameter, which were previously initiated by the RFmxBT Initiate or measurement read VIs. Calling this VI is optional, unless you want to stop a measurement before it is complete. This VI executes even if there is an incoming error.
- [RFmxBT Analyze (IQ, 1 Wfm) VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-analyze-iq-1-wfm-vi.html) Performs the enabled measurements on the I/Q complex waveform that you specify in the IQ parameter. Call this VI after you configure the signal and measurement properties. You can fetch measurement results using the Fetch VIs or result properties in the property node. Use this VI only if the Recommended Acquisition Type property value is either IQ or IQ or Spectral .
- [RFmxBT Create Signal Configuration VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-create-signal-configuration-vi.html) Creates a new instance of a signal.
- [RFmxBT Clone Signal Configuration VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-clone-signal-configuration-vi.html) Creates a new instance of a signal by copying all the property values from an existing signal instance.
- [RFmxBT Delete Signal Configuration VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-delete-signal-configuration-vi.html) Deletes an instance of a signal that you specify in the Signal Name parameter.
- [RFmxBT Get All Named Result Names VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-get-all-named-result-names-vi.html) Returns all the named result names of the signal that you specify in the Selector String parameter.
- [RFmxBT Clear Named Result VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-clear-named-result-vi.html) Clears a result instance specified by the result name in the Selector String parameter.
- [RFmxBT Clear All Named Results VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-clear-all-named-results-vi.html) Clears all results for the signal that you specify in the Selector String parameter.

Parent topic:

Bluetooth

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/rfmx-bt-mx-fetch-mnu.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00011: Fetch

- bundle_id: `rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/rfmx-bt-mx-fetch-mnu.html`

- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the VIs on this palette to fetch Bluetooth measurement results and traces. icon

### Fetch

Use the VIs on this palette to fetch Bluetooth measurement results and traces.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='rfmx-bt-mx-fetch-mnu.png']

- [RFmxBT ModAcc Fetch VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-modacc-fetch-vi.html) Fetches the ModAcc measurement results.
- [RFmxBT ACP Fetch VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-acp-fetch-vi.html) Fetches the ACP measurement results.
- [RFmxBT 20dBBandwidth Fetch VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-20dbbandwidth-fetch-vi.html) Fetches the 20dBBandwidth measurement results.
- [RFmxBT FrequencyRange Fetch VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-frequencyrange-fetch-vi.html) Fetches the FrequencyRange measurement results.
- [RFmxBT TXP Fetch VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-txp-fetch-vi.html) Fetches the TXP measurement results.
- [RFmxBT ModSpectrum Fetch Spectrum VI](../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-modspectrum-fetch-spectrum-vi.html) Fetches the ModSpectrum spectrum trace.
- [Build String](../../../../../menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/utility/rfmx-bt-mx-utility-build-string-mnu.html) Use the VIs on this palette to create strings for configurations and results that require a selector string.

Parent topic:

Bluetooth

- bundle_id: `rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref`

### Utility

Use the VIs on this palette to configure utility VIs.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='dir-mnu.png']

- [RFmxBT Commit VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-commit-vi.html) Commits settings to the hardware. Calling this VI is optional. RFmxBT commits settings to the hardware when you call the RFmxBT Initiate VI or any of the measurement Read VIs.
- [RFmxBT Reset to Default VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-reset-to-default-vi.html) Resets a signal to the default values.
- [RFmxBT Wait for Measurement Complete VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-wait-for-measurement-complete-vi.html) Waits for the specified number for seconds for all the measurements to complete.
- [RFmxBT Check Measurement Status VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-check-measurement-status-vi.html) Checks the status of the measurement. Use this VI to check for any errors that may occur during measurement or to check whether the measurement is complete and results are available.

Parent topic:

Bluetooth

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref path=menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/utility/rfmx-bt-mx-utility-build-string-mnu.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00013: Build String

- bundle_id: `rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/utility/rfmx-bt-mx-utility-build-string-mnu.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/menus/categories/measurement/rfmx/bt/utility/rfmx-bt-mx-utility-build-string-mnu.html
- document_id: `rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the VIs on this palette to create strings for configurations and results that require a selector string. icon

### Build String

Use the VIs on this palette to create strings for configurations and results that require a selector string.

[IMAGE alt='icon' src='rfmx-bt-mx-utility-build-string-mnu.png']

- [RFmxBT Build Signal String VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-build-signal-string-vi.html) Creates a selector string.
- [RFmxBT Build Offset String VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-build-offset-string-vi.html) Creates the offset string.
- [RFmxBT Build Slot String VI](../../../../../../vi-lib/rfmx/bt/mx/rfmxbt-llb/rfmxbt-build-slot-string-vi.html) Creates the slot string for use with the TXP configuration or fetch properties and VIs.

Parent topic:

Fetch

Parent topic:

Bluetooth

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref path=resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt-p.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00014: RFmxBT Properties

- bundle_id: `rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt-p.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt-p.html
- document_id: `rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Use the RFmxBluetooth properties to access options for configuring and fetching measurements. © 2019–2026 National Instruments Corporation. All rights reserved.

### RFmxBT Properties

Use the RFmxBluetooth properties to access options for configuring and fetching measurements.

© 2019–2026 National Instruments Corporation. All rights reserved.

- [20dBBandwidth:All Traces Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb02004.html) Specifies whether to enable all the traces for the 20dBBandwidth measurement.
- [20dBBandwidth:Averaging:Count](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb02003.html) Specifies the number of acquisitions used for averaging when you set the 20dBBandwidth Averaging Enabled property to True .
- [20dBBandwidth:Averaging:Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb02002.html) Specifies whether to enable averaging for the 20dBBandwidth measurement.
- [20dBBandwidth:Measurement Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb02000.html) Specifies whether to enable the 20dBBandwidth measurement specified in section 4.5.5 of the Bluetooth Test Specification RF.TS.p33 . The measurement uses a span of 3 MHz internally. This measurement is valid only for basic rate (BR) packets.
- [20dBBandwidth:Number of Analysis Threads](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb02005.html) Specifies the maximum number of threads used for parallelism for the 20dB bandwidth measurement.
- [20dBBandwidth:Results:Bandwidth (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb02008.html) Returns the 20dB bandwidth of the received signal. It is computed as the difference between 20dBBandwidth Results High Freq and 20dBBandwidth Results Low Freq. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [20dBBandwidth:Results:High Frequency (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb02009.html) Returns the highest frequency above the center frequency at which the transmit power drops 20 dB below the peak power. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [20dBBandwidth:Results:Low Frequency (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0200a.html) Returns the lowest frequency below the center frequency at which the transmit power drops 20 dB below the peak power. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [20dBBandwidth:Results:Peak Power (dBm)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb02007.html) Returns the peak power of the measured spectrum. This value is expressed in dBm.
- [ACP:All Traces Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb05007.html) Specifies whether to enable all traces for the adjacent channel power (ACP) measurements.
- [ACP:Averaging:Count](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb05006.html) Specifies the number of acquisitions used for averaging when you set the ACP Averaging Enabled property to True .
- [ACP:Averaging:Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb05005.html) Specifies whether to enable averaging for the ACP measurement.
- [ACP:Burst Synchronization Type](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb05012.html) Specifies the type of synchronization used for detecting the start of the EDR packet in the adjacent channel power (ACP) measurement.
- [ACP:Measurement Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb05000.html) Specifies whether to enable the ACP measurement.
- [ACP:Number of Analysis Threads](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb05008.html) Specifies the maximum number of threads used for parallelism for adjacent channel power (ACP) measurement.
- [ACP:Number of Offsets](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb05003.html) Specifies the number of offset channels used on either side of the reference channel for the adjacent channel power (ACP) measurement when you set the ACP Offset Channel Mode property to Symmetric . This property also returns the actual number of offsets used in the ACP measurement when you set the ACP Offset Channel Mode property to In-band .
- [ACP:Offset Channel Mode](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb05002.html) Specifies which offset channels are used for the measurement.
- [ACP:Offset Frequency (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb05004.html) Returns the frequency of the offset channel with respect to the reference channel frequency. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [ACP:Reference Channel Bandwidth](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb05015.html)
- [ACP:Reference Channel Bandwidth Mode](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb05016.html)
- [ACP:Results:Lower Offset:Absolute Power (dBm)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0500c.html) Returns the absolute power measured in the lower offset channel. This value is expressed in dBm.
- [ACP:Results:Lower Offset:Margin (dB)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0500e.html) Returns the margin from the limit specified by the mask with exception for lower offsets. This value is expressed in dB. Margin is defined as the difference between the offset absolute power and mask with exception. This result is valid only if you set the ACP Offset Channel Mode property to In-band . This property returns NaN if you set the ACP Offset Channel Mode property to Symmetric .
- [ACP:Results:Lower Offset:Relative Power (dB)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0500d.html) Returns the relative power in the lower offset channel measured with respect to the reference channel power. This value is expressed in dB.
- [ACP:Results:Measurement Status](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0500a.html) Indicates the overall measurement status based on the measurement limits specified by the standard when you set the ACP Offset Channel Mode property to In-band .
- [ACP:Results:Reference Channel Power (dBm)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0500b.html) Returns the power measured over the bandwidth as defined in the Bluetooth standard defined test cases: ACP, EDR In-Band Emission, and LE In-Band Emission at the transmit channel. This value is expressed in dBm.
- [ACP:Results:Upper Offset:Absolute Power (dBm)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0500f.html) Returns the absolute power measured in the upper offset channel. This value is expressed in dBm.
- [ACP:Results:Upper Offset:Margin (dB)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb05011.html) Returns the margin from the limit specified by the mask with exception for upper offsets. This value is expressed in dB. Margin is defined as the difference between the offset absolute power and mask with exception. This result is valid only if you set the ACP Offset Channel Mode property to In-band . This property returns NaN if you set the ACP Offset Channel Mode property to Symmetric .
- [ACP:Results:Upper Offset:Relative Power (dB)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb05010.html) Returns the relative power in the upper offset channel measured with respect to the reference channel power. This value is expressed in dB.
- [Advanced:Auto Level Initial Reference Level (dBm)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0d001.html) Specifies the initial reference level which the RFmxBT Auto Level VI uses to estimate the peak power of the input signal. This value is expressed in dBm.
- [Advanced:Limited Configuration Change](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0d000.html) Specifies the set of properties that are considered by RFmx in the locked signal configuration state.
- [Auto Detect Signal:Detected Data Rate](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0002a.html) Returns the data rate detected by the RFmxBT Auto Detect Signal VI. This property returns a valid data rate only if the Detected Packet Type property returns LE and LE-HDT. This property can be queried only after calling the RFmxBT Auto Detect Signal VI.
- [Auto Detect Signal:Detected Packet Format](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00043.html) Returns the LE High Data Throughput (LE HDT) packet format detected by the RFmxBT Auto Detect Signal VI. This property returns a valid packet format only if the Detected Packet Type property returns LE-HDT. This property can be queried only after calling the RFmxBT Auto Detect Signal VI.
- [Auto Detect Signal:Detected Packet Type](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00019.html) Returns the packet type detected by the RFmxBT Auto Detect Signal VI. This property can be queried only after calling the RFmxBT Auto Detect Signal VI.
- [Auto Detect Signal:Detected Payload Length](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0002b.html) Returns the payload length detected by the RFmxBT Auto Detect Signal VI. This property can be queried only after calling the RFmxBT Auto Detect Signal VI.
- [Center Frequency (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00001.html) Specifies the expected carrier frequency of the RF signal that needs to be acquired. This value is expressed in Hz. The signal analyzer tunes to this frequency.
- [Channel Number](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00017.html) Specifies the RF channel number of the signal generated by the device under test (DUT), as defined in the bluetooth specification. This property is applicable when you enable the ACP measurement and when you set the ACP Offset Channel Mode property to In-band .
- [External Attenuation (dB)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00003.html) Specifies the attenuation of a switch (or cable) connected to the RF IN connector of the signal analyzer. This value is expressed in dB.
- [FrequencyRange:All Traces Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb03005.html) Specifies whether to enable all the traces for FrequencyRange measurement.
- [FrequencyRange:Averaging:Count](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb03004.html) Specifies the number of acquisitions used for averaging when you set the FrequencyRange Averaging Enabled property to True .
- [FrequencyRange:Averaging:Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb03003.html) Specifies whether to enable averaging for the FrequencyRange measurement.
- [FrequencyRange:Measurement Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb03000.html) Specifies whether to enable the FrequencyRange measurement specified in the section 4.5.4 of the Bluetooth Test Specification RF.TS.p33 . This measurement is valid only for basic rate (BR) packets.
- [FrequencyRange:Number of Analysis Threads](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb03006.html) Specifies the maximum number of threads used for parallelism for the frequency range measurement.
- [FrequencyRange:Results:High Frequency (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb03008.html) Returns the highest frequency above the center frequency at which the transmit power drops below -30 dBm measured in a 100 kHz bandwidth. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [FrequencyRange:Results:Low Frequency (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb03009.html) Returns the lowest frequency below the center frequency at which the transmit power drops below -30 dBm measured in a 100 kHz bandwidth. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [FrequencyRange:Span (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb03002.html) Specifies the span for the FrequencyRange measurement. This value is expressed in Hz. You must adjust the span according the center frequency as specified in section 4.5.4 of the Bluetooth Test Specification RF.TS.p33 . It is recommended to use the span of 6 MHz for a center frequency of 2.402 GHz and 10 MHz for a center frequency of 2.48 GHz.
- [ModAcc:All Traces Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04006.html) Specifies whether to enable all the traces computed by ModAcc measurements.
- [ModAcc:Averaging:Count](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04005.html) Specifies the number of acquisitions used for averaging when you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True .
- [ModAcc:Averaging:Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04004.html) Specifies whether to enable averaging for the ModAcc measurements.
- [ModAcc:Burst Synchronization Type](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0402b.html) Specifies the type of synchronization used for detecting the start of packet in ModAcc measurement.
- [ModAcc:Frequency Tracking Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04040.html) Specifies whether to enable frequency tracking for LE- HDT packet. If you set this property to True , the Control Header EVM, Payload EVM, Payload Frequency Error w1 and Frequency Error w0+w1 results are computed after frequency tracking.
- [ModAcc:I/Q Origin Offset Correction Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04003.html) Specifies whether to enable the I/Q origin offset correction for EDR and LE-HDT packets. If you set this property to True , the DEVM and EVM results are computed after correcting for the I/Q origin offset.
- [ModAcc:IQ Mismatch Correction Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0403d.html) Specifies whether to enable the IQ mismatch correction for LE- HDT packet. If you set this property to True , the EVM results are computed after correcting for the IQ gain imbalance and quadrature error .
- [ModAcc:Measurement Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04000.html) Specifies whether to enable the ModAcc measurements. You can use this property to determine the modulation quality of the bluetooth transmitter.
- [ModAcc:Number of Analysis Threads](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04007.html) Specifies the maximum number of threads used for parallelism for the ModAcc measurement. The number of threads can range from 1 to the number of physical cores. The number of threads you set may not be used in calculations. The actual number of threads used depends on the problem size, system resources, data availability, and other considerations.
- [ModAcc:Results:Clock Drift Mean (ppm)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04032.html) Returns the clock drift estimated over the LE-CS packet. This value is expressed in ppm. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the mean of the clock drift values computed for each averaging count.
- [ModAcc:Results:DEVM:99% DEVM (%)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04021.html) Returns the 99th percentile of the differential EVM (DEVM) values computed on symbols of the EDR portion of all measured EDR packets. This value is expressed as a percentage.
- [ModAcc:Results:DEVM:Magnitude Error:Average RMS Magnitude Error Mean (%)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0402d.html) Returns the average of the RMS magnitude error values computed on each 50 us block of EDR portion of the EDR packet. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the mean of the average RMS magnitude error values computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed as a percentage.
- [ModAcc:Results:DEVM:Magnitude Error:Peak RMS Magnitude Error Maximum (%)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0402e.html) Returns the peak of the RMS magnitude error values computed on each 50 us block of EDR portion of the EDR packet. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the maximum of the peak RMS Magnitude error values computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed as a percentage.
- [ModAcc:Results:DEVM:Peak DEVM Maximum (%)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04020.html) Returns the peak of the differential EVM (DEVM) values computed on symbols in the EDR portion of the EDR packet. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the maximum of the peak symbol differential EVM (DEVM) values computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed as a percentage.
- [ModAcc:Results:DEVM:Peak RMS DEVM Maximum (%)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0401e.html) Returns the peak of the RMS differential EVM (DEVM) values computed on each 50us block of the EDR portion of the EDR packet. When you set ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the maximum of the peak RMS differential EVM (DEVM) values computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed as a percentage.
- [ModAcc:Results:DEVM:Percentage of Symbols below 99% DEVM Limit (%)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04022.html) Returns the percentage of symbols in the EDR portion of all the measured EDR packets with differential EVM (DEVM) less than or equal to 99% DEVM threshold as defined in section 4.5.11 of the Bluetooth Test Specification RF.TS.p33. . When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it computes this result using the symbol DEVM values from all averaging counts. This value is expressed as a percentage.
- [ModAcc:Results:DEVM:Phase Error:Average RMS Phase Error Mean (deg)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0402f.html) Return the average of the RMS phase error values computed on each 50 us block of EDR portion of the EDR packet. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the mean of the average RMS phase error values computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in degrees.
- [ModAcc:Results:DEVM:Phase Error:Peak RMS Phase Error Maximum (deg)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04030.html) Return the peak of the RMS phase error values computed on each 50 us block of EDR portion of the EDR packet. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the maximum of the peak RMS phase error values computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in degrees.
- [ModAcc:Results:DEVM:RMS DEVM Mean (%)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0401f.html) Returns the RMS differential EVM (DEVM) value computed on the EDR portion of the EDR packet. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the mean of the RMS differential EVM (DEVM) values computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed as a percentage.
- [ModAcc:Results:EVM:Control Header RMS EVM Mean (dB)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04037.html) Returns the RMS EVM value computed on the control header portion of the LE-HDT packet. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the mean of the RMS EVM values computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in dB. This result is valid only for LE-HDT packet.
- [ModAcc:Results:EVM:Payload RMS EVM Mean (dB)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04038.html) Returns the RMS EVM value computed on the payload portion including the payload header of the LE-HDT packet. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the mean of the RMS EVM values computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in dB. This result is valid only for LE-HDT packet.
- [ModAcc:Results:EVM:Preamble RMS EVM Mean (dB)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04036.html) Returns the RMS EVM value computed on the preamble portion of the LE-HDT packet. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the mean of the RMS EVM values computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in dB. This result is valid only for LE-HDT packet.
- [ModAcc:Results:Fractional Time Offset Mean (s)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04039.html) Returns the fractional time offset value computed on the sounding sequence portion of the LE CS Packet. This value is expressed in seconds. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the mean of the fractional time offset values for each averaging count.
- [ModAcc:Results:Frequency Error:BR:Initial Frequency Error Maximum (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04014.html) Returns the initial frequency error value computed on the preamble portion of the BR packet. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the value corresponding to the maximum of the absolute initial frequency error values computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [ModAcc:Results:Frequency Error:BR:Peak Frequency Drift Maximum (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04015.html) Returns the peak frequency drift value computed on the BR packet. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the value corresponding to the maximum of the absolute peak frequency drift values computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [ModAcc:Results:Frequency Error:BR:Peak Frequency Drift Rate Maximum (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04016.html) Returns the peak frequency drift rate value computed on the BR packet. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the value corresponding to the maximum of the absolute peak frequency drift rate values computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [ModAcc:Results:Frequency Error:EDR:Header Frequency Error wi Maximum (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04017.html) Returns the frequency error value computed on the header of the EDR packet. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the value corresponding to the maximum of the absolute header frequency error values computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [ModAcc:Results:Frequency Error:EDR:Peak Frequency Error w0 Maximum (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04019.html) Returns the peak frequency error value computed on the EDR portion of the EDR packet, relative to the header frequency error. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the value corresponding to the maximum absolute of the peak frequency error values computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [ModAcc:Results:Frequency Error:EDR:Peak Frequency Error wi+w0 Maximum (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04018.html) Returns the peak frequency error value computed on the EDR portion of the EDR packet. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the value corresponding to the maximum of the absolute peak frequency error values computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [ModAcc:Results:Frequency Error:LE-HDT:Frequency Error w0+w1 Maximum (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0403c.html) Returns the total frequency error for the LE-HDT packet. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns a value corresponding to the maximum of the absolute frequency error values computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [ModAcc:Results:Frequency Error:LE-HDT:Payload Frequency Error w1 Maximum (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0403b.html) Returns the frequency error value computed on the payload portion of the LE-HDT packet. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns a value corresponding to the maximum of the absolute payload frequency error values computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [ModAcc:Results:Frequency Error:LE-HDT:Preamble Frequency Error w0 Maximum (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0403a.html) Returns the frequency error value computed on the preamble portion of the LE-HDT packet. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns a value corresponding to the maximum of the absolute preamble frequency error values computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [ModAcc:Results:Frequency Error:LE:Initial Frequency Drift Maximum (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0401b.html) Returns the initial frequency drift value computed on the LE packet. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the value corresponding to the maximum of the absolute initial frequency drift values computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [ModAcc:Results:Frequency Error:LE:Initial Frequency Error Maximum (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04031.html) Returns the initial frequency error value computed on the preamble portion of the LE or LE-CS packet. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns a value corresponding to the maximum of the absolute initial frequency error values computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [ModAcc:Results:Frequency Error:LE:Peak Frequency Drift Maximum (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0401c.html) Returns the peak frequency drift value computed on the LE packet. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the value corresponding to the maximum of the absolute peak frequency drift values computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [ModAcc:Results:Frequency Error:LE:Peak Frequency Drift Rate Maximum (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0401d.html) Returns the peak frequency drift rate value computed on the LE packet. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the value corresponding to the maximum of the absolute peak frequency drift rate values computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [ModAcc:Results:Frequency Error:LE:Peak Frequency Error Maximum (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0401a.html) When you set the Direction Finding Mode property to Disabled , it returns the peak frequency error value computed on the preamble and payload portion of the LE or LE-CS packet. When you set the Direction Finding Mode property to Angle of Arrival , it returns the peak frequency error value computed on the Constant tone extension field of the LE packet. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the value corresponding to the maximum of absolute the peak frequency error values computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [ModAcc:Results:I/Q Origin Offset Mean (dB)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04023.html) Returns the I/Q origin offset estimated over the EDR portion of the EDR packets and preamble portion of the LE-HDT packets. This value is expressed in dB. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the mean of the I/Q origin offset values computed for each averaging count.
- [ModAcc:Results:IQ Gain Imbalance Mean (dB)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0403e.html) Returns the IQ gain imbalance estimated over preamble portion of the LE-HDT packets. This value is expressed in dB. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the mean of the IQ gain imbalance values computed for each averaging count.
- [ModAcc:Results:Preamble Start Time Mean (s)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04033.html) Returns the start time of the preamble of LE-CS packet. This value is expressed in seconds. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the mean of the preamble start time values computed for each averaging count.
- [ModAcc:Results:Quadrature Error Mean (deg)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0403f.html) Returns the quadrature error estimated over preamble portion of the LE-HDT packets. This value is expressed in degree. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the mean of the quadrature error values computed for each averaging count.
- [ModAcc:Results:df1:Minimum df1max Minimum (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0400d.html) Returns the minimum df1max value computed on the signal. The measurement computes df1max deviation values on a packet and reports the minimum value. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the minimum of the Min df1max results computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [ModAcc:Results:df1:Peak df1max Maximum (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0400c.html) Returns the peak df1max value computed on the signal. The measurement computes df1max deviation values on a packet and reports the peak value. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the maximum of the peak df1max results computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [ModAcc:Results:df1:Percentage of Symbols above df1max Threshold (%)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0402c.html) Returns the percentage of symbols with df1max values that are greater than the df1max threshold defined by the standard. This result is valid only for the LE packet with a data rate of 125 Kbps. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it computes this result using the df1max values from all averaging counts. This value expressed as a percentage.
- [ModAcc:Results:df1:df1avg Maximum (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0400a.html) Returns the df1avg value computed on the signal. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the maximum of the df1avg results computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [ModAcc:Results:df1:df1avg Mean (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04009.html) Returns the df1avg value computed on the signal. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the mean of the df1avg results computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in Hz
- [ModAcc:Results:df1:df1avg Minimum (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0400b.html) Returns the df1avg value computed on the signal. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the minimum of the df1avg results computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [ModAcc:Results:df2:Minimum df2max Minimum (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04012.html) Returns the minimum df2max value computed on the signal. The measurement computes df2max deviation values on a packet and reports the minimum value. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the minimum of the Min df2max results computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [ModAcc:Results:df2:Peak df2max Maximum (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04011.html) Returns the peak df2max value computed on the signal. The measurement computes df2max deviation values on a packet and reports the peak value. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the maximum of the peak df2max results computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [ModAcc:Results:df2:Percentage of Symbols above df2max Threshold (%)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04013.html) Returns the percentage of symbols with df2max values that are greater than the df2max threshold defined by the standard. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it computes this result using the df2max values from all averaging counts. This value is expressed as a percentage.
- [ModAcc:Results:df2:df2avg Maximum (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0400f.html) Returns the df2avg value computed on the signal. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the maximum of the df2avg results computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [ModAcc:Results:df2:df2avg Mean (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0400e.html) Returns the df2avg value computed on the signal. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the mean of the df2avg results computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [ModAcc:Results:df2:df2avg Minimum (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04010.html) Returns the df2avg value computed on the signal. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the minimum of the df2avg results computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [ModAcc:Results:df3:df3avg Mean (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04034.html) Returns the df3avg value computed on the signal. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the mean of the df3avg results computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in Hz. This result is valid only for LE-CS packet with data rate 2 Mbps and when bandwidth bit period product is set to 2.
- [ModAcc:Results:df4:Percentage of Symbols above df4avg Threshold (%)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb04035.html) Returns the percentage of symbols with df4avg values that are greater than the df4avg threshold defined by the standard. When you set the ModAcc Averaging Enabled property to True , it computes this result using the df4avg values from all averaging counts. This value is expressed as a percentage. This result is valid only for LE-CS packet with data rate 2 Mbps and when bandwidth bit period product is set to 2.
- [ModSpectrum:All Traces Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0f005.html) Specifies whether to enable all the traces used for ModSpectrum measurements.
- [ModSpectrum:Averaging:Count](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0f004.html) Specifies the number of acquisitions used for averaging when you set the ModSpectrum Averaging Enabled property to True .
- [ModSpectrum:Averaging:Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0f003.html) Specifies whether to enable averaging for ModSpectrum measurements.
- [ModSpectrum:Burst Synchronization Type](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0f002.html) Specifies the type of synchronization used for detecting the start of packet in the ModSpectrum measurement.
- [ModSpectrum:Measurement Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0f000.html) Specifies whether to enable the ModSpectrum measurements.This measurement is valid only for channel sounding (CS) packets.
- [ModSpectrum:Number of Analysis Threads](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0f006.html) Specifies the maximum number of threads used for parallelism for ModSpectrum measurement.
- [ModSpectrum:Results:Bandwidth (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0f008.html) Returns the 6 dB bandwidth of the received signal. It is computed as the difference between ModSpectrum Results High Freq and ModSpectrum Results Low Freq . This value is expressed in Hz.
- [ModSpectrum:Results:High Frequency (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0f009.html) Returns the highest frequency above the center frequency at which the transmit power drops 6dB below the peak power. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [ModSpectrum:Results:Low Frequency (Hz)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0f00a.html) Returns the lowest frequency below the center frequency at which the transmit power drops 6 dB below the peak power. This value is expressed in Hz.
- [Packet:Access Address](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00011.html) Specifies the 32-bit LE access address.
- [Packet:BD Address:LAP](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0000f.html) Specifies the 24-bit lower address part (LAP) of the bluetooth device address (BD_ADDR).
- [Packet:Bandwidth Bit Period Product](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00034.html) Specifies the bandwidth bit period product of GFSK modulation for LE-CS packet type.
- [Packet:Channel Sounding:Antenna Switch Time (s)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00035.html) Specifies the Channel Sounding Antenna Switch Time for the LE-CS packet. This property is applicable only when you set the Packet Type property to LE-CS and the CS Packet Format property to any value other than SYNC .
- [Packet:Channel Sounding:Number of Antenna Path](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00036.html) Specifies the number of antenna paths for the generated LE-CS packet. This property is applicable only when you set the Packet Type property to LE-CS and the CS Packet Format property to any value other than SYNC .
- [Packet:Channel Sounding:Packet Format](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00030.html) Specifies the format of the Channel Sounding packet depending on the position and presence of SYNC and CS Tone fields. This property is applicable only when you set the Packet Type property to LE-CS .
- [Packet:Channel Sounding:Phase Measurement Period](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00032.html) Specifies the Channel Sounding Phase Measurement Period for the LE-CS packet. This property is applicable only when you set the Packet Type property to LE-CS and the CS Packet Format property to any value other than SYNC .
- [Packet:Channel Sounding:SYNC Sequence](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00031.html) Specifies the type of sequence present in the SYNC portion after trailer bits. This property is applicable only when you set the Packet Type property to LE-CS and the CS Packet Format property to any value other than CS Tone .
- [Packet:Channel Sounding:Tone Extension Slot](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00033.html) Specifies whether the tone extension slot transmission is enabled after CS Tone. This property is applicable only when you set the Packet Type property to LE-CS and the CS Packet Format property to any value other than SYNC .
- [Packet:Data Rate (bps)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0000e.html) Specifies the data rate of the LE, LE-CS or LE-HDT packet transmitted by the device under test (DUT). This value is expressed in bps. This property is applicable only to LE, LE-CS or LE-HDT packet type.
- [Packet:Direction Finding:CTE Length (s)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0002d.html) Specifies the length of the constant tone extension (CTE) field in the generated signal. This value is expressed in seconds. This property is applicable only when you set the Direction Finding Mode property to either Angle of Arrival or Angle of Departure .
- [Packet:Direction Finding:CTE Number of Transmit Slots](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0002f.html) Returns the number of transmit slots in the constant time extension portion of the generated LE packet. This property is applicable only when you set the Direction Finding Mode property to Angle of Arrival or Angle of Departure .
- [Packet:Direction Finding:CTE Slot Duration (s)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0002e.html) Specifies the length of the switching slots and transmit slots in the constant tone extension field in the generated signal. This property is applicable only when you set the Direction Finding Mode property to Angle of Arrival or Angle of Departure .
- [Packet:Direction Finding:Mode](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0002c.html) Specifies the mode of direction finding.
- [Packet:High Data Throughput: Packet Format](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00038.html) Specifies the Higher Data Throughput (HDT) packet format. This property is applicable only when you set the Packet Type property to LE-HDT .
- [Packet:High Data Throughput: Zadoff-Chu Index](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00039.html) Specifies Zadoff-Chu Index for the Long Training Sequence in the preamble. Input to the Zadoff-Chu Index property must be in the range of [1 - 16]. This property is applicable only when you set the Packet Type property to LE-HDT .
- [Packet:High Data Throughput:Auto Preamble Detection Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00042.html) Specifies whether to enable the auto-detection of preamble field in the packet. When AutoPreamble Detection Enabled property is set to True, the measurement auto detects the LTS field of the LE-HDT packet and ignores Zadoff-Chu Index property. This property is applicable only when you set the Packet Type property to LE-HDT .
- [Packet:High Data Throughput:Number of Block Repetition Sequences](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00041.html)
- [Packet:High Data Throughput:VHDT Mode Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00040.html)
- [Packet:Payload Bit Pattern](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00012.html) Specifies the bit pattern present in the payload of the packet. This value is used to determine the set of ModAcc measurements to be performed.
- [Packet:Payload Length (bytes)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00014.html) Specifies the payload length of BR, EDR, LE and LE-CS packet, and the payload zone length of LE-HDT packet, in bytes. This property is applicable only when you set the Payload Length Mode property to Manual . This property returns the payload length or payload zone length used for measurement if you set the Payload Length Mode property to Auto .
- [Packet:Payload Length Mode](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00013.html) Specifies the payload length mode of the signal to be measured. The payload length mode and Payload Length properties decide the length of the payload to be used for measurement.
- [Packet:Type](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0000d.html) Specifies the type of the Bluetooth packet to be measured.
- [PowerRamp:Averaging:Count](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0e006.html) Specifies the number of acquisitions used for averaging when you set the PowerRamp Averaging Enabled property to True .
- [PowerRamp:Averaging:Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0e005.html) Specifies whether to enable averaging for PowerRamp measurement.
- [PowerRamp:Burst Synchronization Type](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0e002.html) Specifies the type of synchronization used for detecting the start of packet in the PowerRamp measurement.
- [PowerRamp:Measurement Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0e000.html) Specifies whether to enable PowerRamp measurements. This measurement is valid only for low energy CS (LE-CS) packets.
- [PowerRamp:Number of Analysis Threads](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0e007.html) Specifies the maximum number of threads used for parallelism for PowerRamp measurement.
- [PowerRamp:Results: 40dB Fall Time Mean (s)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0e00b.html) 40dB Fall Time returns the fall time of the acquired signal at which transmit power drops 40 dB below average power. When you set the PowerRamp Averaging Enabled property to True , this parameter returns the mean of the 40dB fall time computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in seconds.
- [PowerRamp:Results:Fall Time Mean (s)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0e00a.html) Fall Time returns the fall time of the acquired signal that is the amount of time taken for the power envelope to fall from a level of 90 percent to 10 percent. When you set the PowerRamp Averaging Enabled property to True ,this parameter returns the mean of the fall time computed for each averaging countt. This value is expressed in seconds.
- [PowerRamp:Results:Rise Time Mean (s)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0e009.html) Rise Time returns the rise time of the acquired signal that is the amount of time taken for the power envelope to rise from a level of 10 percent to 90 percent. When you set the PowerRamp Averaging Enabled property to True , this parameter returns the mean of the rise time computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in seconds.
- [Reference Level](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00002.html) Specifies the reference level that represents the maximum expected power of the RF input signal. This value is expressed in dBm for RF devices and Vpk-pk for baseband devices.
- [Reference Level Headroom](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00ffc.html) Specifies the margin RFmx adds to the Reference Level property. The margin avoids clipping and overflow warnings if the input signal exceeds the configured reference level.
- [Result Fetch Timeout (s)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0c000.html) Specifies the time, in seconds, to wait before results are available in the RFmxBT Property Node . Set this value to a time longer than expected for fetching the measurement. A value of -1 specifies that the RFmxBT Property Node waits until the measurement is complete.
- [Selected Ports](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00ffd.html) Specifies the instrument port to be configured to acquire a signal. Use RFmxInstr Get Available Ports VI to get the valid port names.
- [Selector String](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00000.html) Specifies the active channel string used to access all subsequent channel-based properties in this instance of the property node.
- [TXP:All Traces Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb01004.html) Specifies whether to enable all the traces used for transmit power (TxP) measurements.
- [TXP:Averaging:Count](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb01003.html) Specifies the number of acquisitions used for averaging when you set the TXP Averaging Enabled property to True .
- [TXP:Averaging:Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb01002.html) Specifies whether to enable averaging for the transmit power (TxP) measurements.
- [TXP:Burst Synchronization Type](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb01010.html) Specifies the type of synchronization used for detecting the start of packet in the transmit power (TXP) measurement.
- [TXP:Measurement Enabled](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb01000.html) Specifies whether to enable the transmit power (TxP) measurements.
- [TXP:Number of Analysis Threads](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb01005.html) Specifies the maximum number of threads used for parallelism for TXP measurement.
- [TXP:Results:Average Power Maximum (dBm)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb01008.html) Returns the average power computed over the measurement interval. When you set the Direction Finding Mode property to Angle of Departure for LE packets, it will exclude guard period and all the switching slots for the average power computation. For LE-HDT, average power is calculated from beginning of the payload portion. When you set the TXP Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the maximum of the average power results computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in dBm.
- [TXP:Results:Average Power Mean (dBm)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb01007.html) Returns the average power computed over the measurement interval. When you set the Direction Finding Mode property to Angle of Departure for LE packets, it will exclude guard period and all the switching slots for the average power computation. For LE-HDT, average power is calculated from beginning of the payload portion. This value is expressed in dBm. When you set the TXP Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the mean of the average power results computed for each averaging count.
- [TXP:Results:Average Power Minimum (dBm)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb01009.html) Returns the average power computed over the measurement interval. When you set the Direction Finding Mode property to Angle of Departure for LE packets, it will exclude guard period and all the switching slots for the average power computation. For LE-HDT, average power is calculated from beginning of the payload portion. When you set the TXP Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the minimum of the average power results computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in dBm.
- [TXP:Results:EDR DPSK Average Power Mean (dBm)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0100d.html) Returns the average power of the DPSK portion of the EDR packet. When you set the TXP Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the mean of the DPSK average power results computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in dBm.
- [TXP:Results:EDR DPSK GFSK Average Power Ratio Mean (dB)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb01013.html) Returns the ratio of the average power of the DPSK portion to the average power of the GFSK portion of the EDR packet. When you set the TXP Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the mean of the DPSK GFSK average power ratio results computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in dB.
- [TXP:Results:EDR GFSK Average Power Mean (dBm)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0100c.html) Returns the average power of the GFSK portion of the EDR packet. When you set the TXP Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the mean of the GFSK average power results computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in dBm.
- [TXP:Results:LE CS Phase Measurement Period Average Power Mean (dBm)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb01018.html) Returns the average power computed over each antenna path during phase measurement period of the LE-CS packet. This result is applicable only when you set the Packet Type property to LE-CS and the CS Packet Format property to any value other than SYNC . When you set the TXP Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the mean of the phase measurement period average power results computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in dBm.
- [TXP:Results:LE CTE Reference Period Average Power Mean (dBm)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb01014.html) Returns the average power computed over the reference period in the CTE portion of the LE packet. This result is applicable only when you set the Direction Finding Mode property to Angle of Departure . When you set the TXP Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the mean of the CTE reference period average power results computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in dBm.
- [TXP:Results:LE CTE Reference Period Peak Absolute Power Deviation Maximum (%)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb01015.html) Returns the peak absolute power deviation computed over the reference period in the CTE portion of the LE packet. The peak absolute power deviation is the deviation of peak power with respect to the average power in the reference period. This result is applicable only when you set the Direction Finding Mode property to Angle of Departure . When you set the TXP Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the maximum of the CTE reference period absolute power deviation results computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed as a percentage.
- [TXP:Results:LE CTE Transmit Slot Average Power Mean (dBm)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb01016.html) Returns the average power computed over each transmit slot in CTE portion of the LE packet. This result is applicable only when you set the Direction Finding Mode property to Angle of Departure . When you set the TXP Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the mean of the CTE transmit slot average power results computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in dBm.
- [TXP:Results:LE CTE Transmit Slot Peak Absolute Power Deviation Maximum (%)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb01017.html) Returns the peak absolute power deviation computed over each transmit slot in the CTE portion of the LE packet. The peak absolute power deviation is the deviation of peak power in each transmit slot with respect to the average power in that transmit slot. This result is applicable only when you set the Direction Finding Mode property to Angle of Departure . When you set the TXP Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the maximum of the CTE transmit slot absolute power deviation results computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed as a percentage.
- [TXP:Results:Peak Power Maximum (dBm)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0100a.html) Returns the peak power computed over the measurement interval. When you set the Direction Finding Mode property to Angle of Departure for LE packets, it will exclude guard period and all the switching slots for the peak power computation. When you set the TXP Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the maximum of the peak power results computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in dBm.
- [TXP:Results:Peak to Average Power Ratio Maximum (dB)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0100b.html) Returns the peak to average power ratio computed over the measurement interval. When you set the Direction Finding Mode property to Angle of Departure for LE packets, it will exclude guard period and all the switching slots for the peak to average power ratio computation. For LE-HDT, PAPR is calculated using peak power calculated over active portion of burst and average power calculated from beginning of the payload portion. When you set the TXP Averaging Enabled property to True , it returns the maximum of the peak to average power ratio results computed for each averaging count. This value is expressed in dB.
- [Trigger:Delay (s)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0000a.html) Specifies the trigger delay time. This value is expressed in seconds.
- [Trigger:Digital Edge:Edge](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00006.html) Specifies the active edge for the trigger. This property is valid only when you set the Trigger Type property to Digital Edge .
- [Trigger:Digital Edge:Source](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00005.html) Specifies the source terminal for the digital edge trigger. This property is used only when you set the Trigger Type property to Digital Edge .
- [Trigger:IQ Power Edge:Level (dB or dBm)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00008.html) Specifies the power level at which the device triggers. The device asserts the trigger when the signal exceeds the level specified by the value of this parameter, taking into consideration the specified slope.
- [Trigger:IQ Power Edge:Level Type](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00fff.html) Specifies the reference for the IQ Power Edge Level property. The IQ Power Edge Level Type property is used only when you set the Trigger Type property to IQ Power Edge .
- [Trigger:IQ Power Edge:Slope](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00009.html) Specifies whether the device asserts the trigger when the signal power is rising or when it is falling. The device asserts the trigger when the signal power exceeds the specified level with the slope you specify. This property is used only when you set the Trigger Type property to IQ Power Edge .
- [Trigger:IQ Power Edge:Source](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00007.html) Specifies the channel from which the device monitors the trigger. This property is valid only when you set the Trigger Type property to IQ Power Edge .
- [Trigger:Minimum Quiet Time:Duration (s)](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0000c.html) Specifies the time duration for which the signal must be quiet before the signal analyzer arms the I/Q power edge trigger. This value is expressed in seconds.
- [Trigger:Minimum Quiet Time:Mode](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb0000b.html) Specifies whether the measurement computes the minimum quiet time used for triggering.
- [Trigger:Type](../../../resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00004.html) Specifies the type of trigger to be used for signal acquisition.

## TOPIC 00016: Center Frequency (Hz)

- bundle_id: `rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00001.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00001.html
- document_id: `rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the expected carrier frequency of the RF signal that needs to be acquired. This value is expressed in Hz. The signal analyzer tunes to this frequency. You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the Selector Strings

### Center Frequency (Hz)

Specifies the expected carrier frequency of the RF signal that needs to be acquired. This value is expressed in Hz. The signal analyzer tunes to this frequency.

You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the [Selector Strings](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) topic for information about the string syntax for named signals.

The default value is hardware dependent. The default value for the devices PXIe-5645/5820 is 0 Hz. The default value for devices PXIe-5644/5646/5840/5663/5663E/5665/5668R is 2.402 GHz.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | Center Freq (Hz) |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| Resettable | Yes |

## TOPIC 00019: Trigger:Type

- bundle_id: `rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref`
- source_path: `resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00004.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/resource/objmgr/rfmxbt-rc/rfmxbt/attrb00004.html
- document_id: `rfmxbluetooth-labview-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the type of trigger to be used for signal acquisition. You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the Selector Strings topic for information about the string syntax for named signals. The default value is IQ Power E

### Trigger:Type

Specifies the type of trigger to be used for signal acquisition.

You do not need to use a selector string to configure or read this property for the default signal instance. Refer to the [Selector Strings](/csh?context=rfmxspecan_rfmxspecan_selector_string) topic for information about the string syntax for named signals.

The default value is **IQ Power Edge**.

#### Remarks

The following table lists the [characteristics](/csh?productcategories=147794&context=lvcore_lvprop_flags) of this property.

| Short Name | Trigger Type |
| --- | --- |
| Data type |  |
| Permissions | Read/Write |
| Resettable | Yes |

| None | 0 | No reference trigger is used for signal acquisition. |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Digital Edge | 1 | A digital-edge trigger is used for signal acquisition. The source of the digital edge is specified using the Digital Edge Source property. |
| IQ Power Edge | 2 | An I/Q power-edge trigger is used for signal acquisition, which is configured using the IQ Power Edge Slope property. |
| Software | 3 | A software trigger is used for signal acquisition. |

Parent topic:

RFmxBT Properties

| PXI_Trig6 | PXI_Trig6 | The trigger is received on PXI trigger line 6. |
| PXI_Trig7 | PXI_Trig7 | The trigger is received on PXI trigger line 7. |

| PXIe_DStarB | PXIe_DStarB | The trigger is received on the PXIe DStar B trigger line. This value is valid only on the PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860. |
| TimerEvent | TimerEvent | The trigger is received from the Timer event. This value is valid only on the PXIe-5820/5840/5841/5842/5860 and for digital edge Advance Triggers on the PXIe-5663E/5665. |
| PulseIn | PulseIn | The trigger is received from the PULSE IN terminal. This value is valid only on the PXIe-5842. |
| DIO/PFI0 | DIO/PFI0 | The trigger is received on PFI 0 of the DIO front panel connector. |
